IOTA Addresses frozen due to key reuse

As detailed in this forum post, in September the IOTA foundation decided to "freeze" iota tokens on addresses which were reused so often that it was possible for attackers to guess the private key.

A similar incident occured at end of Ocrober, where more addresses were frozen

If you want to know if you are affected (or if you are unable to get your balance back even after adding many addresses) search for your addresses in the list below (sorted by balance).

If you find anything, you will have to use the claim process include in wallet 2.5.2 or later. After claiming, wait for further instructions from the IOTA foundation.

Claim processing has started now. Addresses marked in bold below require KYC before claims can be processed (see this blog post).
